It is reported that the store owner presented the original letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Zhabei Fifth District Headquarters, and the General Bureau Inspectorate, requesting an investigation. The warning letter is as follows:

"Pacific Pharmacy, be informed! We have found that you are privately dealing with the enemy, selling a large number of enemy goods disguised as silk, deceiving the public. It is truly hateful! You are Chinese, how can you not know that 'September 18th,' 'January 28th,' and the three northeastern provinces have been occupied by the enemy? Our team has discovered your extremely evil behavior, disregarding the loss of the country, only seeking profit, and using economic means to assist the enemy. We hope you wake up quickly and seal up and clear out the enemy goods. Now we are giving you a small gift as a warning. If you continue to be stubborn, we will take drastic measures against you, etc." The letter also has a drawing of a pistol, a knife, and a human heart. The letter is stamped with a triangular seal, engraved with "China People's xx xx xx xx xx (these five characters are unclear) Special Task Force."

Wen Ying's Mother Appeals Against Diao Ao Ke 133

Seduction First, Murder Later

Request for Compensation for All Losses

Since the female physiognomist Wen Ying was murdered by her lover Fan Hongsheng, the police arrested Fan, and he was sentenced and imprisoned in the Tilanqiao Western Prison. Last month, she filed a criminal complaint against the three, accusing them of offenses against public morals. The First Special District Court concluded the initial trial, finding the evidence insufficient and acquitting Cheng and the others. This has been reported in previous newspapers. However, Huang Wu insisted that Cheng Meixian seduced her daughter first, then incited her murder, that Cheng Lingqing induced her daughter to prostitution, and that Feng Mengyun was an accomplice. All these facts were the cause of death. She could not accept the initial trial's acquittal of the three and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, requesting the original verdict be overturned and a thorough investigation be conducted to redress the grievance. She also argued that her daughter had completed her apprenticeship and was able to support her in her old age. Since she was murdered, the defendants should be ordered to compensate for all losses. Yesterday, three judges from the Second Branch of the High Court, Zhao, Zhou, and Jiang, formed a collegial panel to hear the case, with Judge Zhao serving as the presiding judge. First, they asked the appellant, Huang Wu, about the purpose of the appeal. Because she could not afford to hire a lawyer, she recounted in detail the circumstances of her daughter's encounter with Cheng Meixian (Diao Ao Ke) in Hangzhou. Cheng saw that her daughter was beautiful and, using the pretext of teaching her photography, lured her to Shanghai. Later, she came to Shanghai to see her daughter.

The Largest Morphine and Red Pill Operation in the French Concession 134

Secretly Manufactured on Rooftop Terraces at Night

Workers Suspended Up and Down with Thick Hemp Ropes

││ French Police Conduct a Thorough Search and Arrest Eight People ││

Yesterday, this newspaper published a news item titled "Large-Scale Neighborhood Search Last Night." At about 10 PM the night before last, the French police suddenly mobilized all Chinese and Western detectives on duty and surrounded Zhengjia Muqiao Street near Avenue Edward VII. They arrested more than ten men and women. Until about 2 AM yesterday morning, Chinese and Western detectives were still stationed at the entrance of the alley. Upon hearing the news, a reporter personally went to investigate. Seeing the detectives guarding the entrance, the situation seemed very serious. In addition, the newspaper was about to go to press, so the reporter hurriedly returned to the office to write the story. However, it was expected that the case must be significant. It turns out that Zhang Zonghan, a Ningbo native, started his career by dealing in white goods and morphine. His main manufacturing operation was originally located in the International Settlement, but due to strict searches, he could not gain a foothold. He moved to No. 15 Bulinli, Zhengjia Muqiao Street in the French Concession. The house is a three-story building with three rooms on top and three rooms below. He used the rooftop terrace and hired craftsmen to build four main rooms on the roof, installing motors and machinery. Every night, he secretly manufactured morphine and red pills. To avoid being seen, the workers used thick hemp ropes for going up and down instead of stairs. The mechanism was extremely ingenious, but it was eventually discovered by the special investigation officers of the French police, Jin Jiulin, Yao Jinfu, and Su Shichi, etc. At 10:15 PM the night before last, they led chief detective Zhang Ziying, detectives Wang Zhihao, Xue Youlin, Zhu Judong, etc., along with Western Chief Detective Xiao Peishi (transliteration) and Western Deputy Detective Xiang Tuolai (transliteration), etc., to the address. They charged straight to the third floor, climbed up the rope, and found the rooftop operation brightly lit. The workers were working on the manufacturing. On the spot, they arrested Yu Jinfu (27 years old, Ningbo native), Zhou Xuewen (32 years old, Yixing native), Ye Ronggen (32 years old, Ningbo native), Fei Xiangfu (28 years old, Ningbo native), Wang A'er (32 years old, Tongzhou native), Jiang A'si (37 years old, Tongzhou native), Wu Mingsheng (42 years old, Ningbo native), and seven others, as well as a Ningbo woman, Chen Li (28 years old), downstairs, for a total of eight people. The main culprit, Zhang Zonghan, happened to be out and was not caught. Twelve bags of raw morphine materials were confiscated. The search was completed by dawn. The police first took Yu and the others to the police station, then sent detectives to guard the operation and hired craftsmen to dismantle the machinery. The total value of the confiscated machinery and raw materials is estimated at about 100,000 yuan. This is the largest morphine and red pill operation broken in the French Concession. Yesterday afternoon, the police sent Yu and the others to the Second Special District Court for investigation. At 3 PM, Criminal Division Chief Wang Wangxu took the bench in the Criminal Division One. The police lawyer, Fei Xizhen, stated that the police had not yet investigated the case and that the main culprit was still at large. He requested a postponement and that the defendants be detained temporarily pending a detailed investigation and the arrest of the main culprit, before filing a lawsuit. Detective Wang Zhihao then reported on the circumstances of the raid and the arrest of the defendants, and presented the twelve bags of morphine to the court. The court verified the report and questioned the defendants before ordering a postponement until the 15th for further questioning. The defendants were returned to the police station for detention. × × × × × ×

County Slaughter Tax Contract Bidding 140

Appeal from the Minhang Preserved Fresh Food Industry Association

The Shanghai County Government has received an order from the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office, which states in brief: "It is found that the term for contracting the slaughter tax in the county expires at the end of July this year. In accordance with the regulations, bidding should be carried out first to increase educational funds. It is scheduled to set up a bidding box in the county government hall on July 12 for merchants to submit bids. The public should be widely informed, and bidding vouchers should be prepared in advance for merchants to collect and submit bids. The names and tax amounts of the merchants with the highest bids should be reported for verification. In addition to the supervision of committee member Wu Jiaxu, it should be notified to all," etc. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Cao announced to the merchants in the county that the slaughter tax for this term would also include a special construction donation, which is one-quarter of the regular tax. The Minhang Preserved Fresh Food Industry Association of Shanghai County sent a letter to the authorities stating: "To the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office and the Shanghai County Government, We respectfully submit: It is found that since the county's

slaughter tax has been contracted through bidding, contractors, for the sake of personal gain, do not hesitate to increase the bid amount to achieve the purpose of contracting. The increased bid amount, as well as salaries and public expenses, are all based on the authority to collect from meat merchants. The winning bidder does not need to compensate, and the burden on the meat industry becomes heavier, while the contractor's income becomes more abundant, and the suffering of the meat industry deepens.

The contractor's profits are therefore thick. It is found that the towns in the county are completely rural market gatherings. The prosperity of trade is based on the amount of consumption by farmers. In addition to the continuous years of drought, they have also suffered from the impact of cheap sales hurting farmers. The rural economy has fallen into bankruptcy, and farmers' expenses are shrinking everywhere, especially fresh meat, which is at the top of the list of savings. Trade is sluggish, and they are losing money. The two-year slaughter tax has been contracted by people outside the industry who do not know the actual plight of meat merchants. The bid is huge, and they do not consider whether the meat industry can bear it. It is now heard that this year's slaughter tax has a minimum amount of 3,800 yuan and is scheduled to be bid on July 12. In order to avoid exploitation by contractors and relieve the suffering of meat merchants, the industry association, in accordance with the precedents of the Shanghai city, still bids at a low amount, or in accordance with the previous year's Ding and Chen bid amount, is responsible for recognizing and handling the bid, fairly distributing the burden, and each district painfully pays it, eliminating the contractor's ambition and extortion, reducing the pain of the meat industry's extra burden. There is no need to worry about any shortfall in the special education fund. As for cash deposits and guarantee procedures, etc., once instructions are received, they will be paid in accordance with the regulations. The date of payment will be determined separately by representatives who will collect and deliver on time. The urgent telegram is infinitely sincere and awaiting orders. During the industry's request period, please postpone the bidding temporarily. If a contractor bids a huge amount, the extra tax should be borne and reported by the bidder himself, and the industry association will never recognize it. This is all stated together. The Minhang Preserved Fresh Food Industry Association of Shanghai County bows."

Sudden Water Outage in Hengtai Lane 143

Tenants' Association Negotiates with Both Parties

According to the Hua Dong News Agency, the Hengtai Lane area of Zhoujiazui, Hongkou, suddenly had its water supply cut off by the Shanghai Waterworks Company yesterday, causing panic among the tenants in the lane. They immediately reported it to the Tenants' Association, which sent representatives such as Wang Shoushen to negotiate with the company. The company's representatives stated that the landlord, Hengtai Company, was more than six months in arrears on water bills. In order to maintain operations, the company had no choice but to take this measure, so the representatives should negotiate with the landlord. The representatives immediately phoned the landlord to question them and demanded that they pay the water bills immediately to avoid further disputes. However, the landlord, Hengtai Company, claimed that the water bills had suddenly increased and that they had no funds to pay. The issue remained unresolved. The representatives had no choice but to renegotiate with the waterworks company, requesting a postponement of the water cutoff so that tenants who had paid their rent and water bills would not suffer. The company agreed to do so but stated that the landlord must pay the water bills within five days; otherwise, the water cutoff would continue. The representatives expressed their satisfaction. That evening, an emergency meeting of all tenants was called by the Tenants' Association in the lane. It was decided that: 1) Representatives such as Wang Shoushen would directly negotiate with the landlord, demanding that they pay the water bills immediately; 2) Each household would be levied three yuan to cover the costs of negotiation, which would not be refunded; 3) Letters would be sent to the Municipal People's Association, the General Tenants' Association, and party and government organs, requesting assistance; 4) Legal counsel would be hired. The meeting was then adjourned.

Therefore, the Western Restaurants, Hotels, Candy, Biscuit, and Tea Food Associations have jointly sent letters to the Ministry of Finance, the Taxation Department, and the Stamp Tax Bureau, earnestly urging her retention. The letter stated: "To whom it may concern, we, the members of our associations, have learned that Ms. Wen Yongshu, the stamp tax salesperson for the 4th and 5th districts of the Special District, has been ordered to be dismissed and reassigned. Our members are greatly surprised. The stamp tax has not been implemented in the concessions for long. At the beginning, the emphasis was on encouragement. Over the past five or six years, thanks to Ms. Wen's hard work and earnest encouragement, merchants gradually complied with affixing the stamps, leading to increased sales and sufficient tax revenue. The authorities should commend her to show appreciation for her hard work. Instead, she is being dismissed, which our members find incomprehensible. We request that you promptly send a letter to the authorities, earnestly urging her retention, to avoid losing a virtuous public servant who fosters cooperation between officials and merchants." It further stated that since Ms. Wen assumed office, she has worked diligently and selflessly, maintaining her integrity and never engaging in corruption. She has earned the trust of merchants, and the widespread adoption of stamp tax in the concessions is indeed due to her efforts over the past five or six years. Now, the Jiangsu Stamp Tax and Excise Bureau is not only failing to reward her but also dismissing her, which greatly alarms the business community. For the sake of the country's tax revenue and the merchants' trust, we hereby earnestly request that your department order the Jiangsu Stamp Tax and Excise Bureau to immediately rescind its order and safeguard national taxes. The nation will be fortunate, and the business community will be fortunate. We hereby inform you and hope you will investigate accordingly. Respectfully submitted to Director Xie of the Taxation Department, Ministry of Finance."

It will also provide emergency medicine for epidemic diseases. It is hoped that people will direct those suffering from diseases to seek treatment, as it will be a great merit.

│Deceased Had Elderly Father, Situation Extremely Tragic│

Zhu Ronghai, 41 years old from Haimen, lived at 29 Yaojiazhai Bridge, Zhabei. He had an elderly father to support. Zhu earned a living by cutting hair for people along the road. His daily income was meager, resulting in an extremely impoverished family situation. At approximately 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, Zhu was walking alone along Gordon Road and Avenue Road, from east to west, intending to cross the road when a soldier named Si Dai Ai (transliteration) of the United States Marine Corps stationed at 50 Haifang Road, was driving motorcycle number 1876, speeding from south to north. Unable to avoid the collision, Zhu was knocked to the ground and suffered severe head injuries. A Chinese patrolman with badge number 2989 witnessed the incident and immediately reported it to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, which dispatched investigators. The injured man was sent to the Red Cross Hospital, where he died. The body was taken to the Philan Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. During the inquest, Si Dai Ai testified that he was driving north along Gordon Road, and the deceased was walking east to west. The deceased had already crossed his vehicle when another car approached from the north. Seeing that car, he walked back, and he was unable to stop in time, causing the collision. Zhu Chunjin, the father of the deceased, testified that he only had one son, whose livelihood he depended on. Now that he had been killed, he did not know what to do. He intended to transport the body back to his hometown, but he had no money to pay for the coffin. He broke down in tears, his situation being extremely tragic. After hearing the testimony, Guo ordered an examination of the deceased, Zhu Ronghai, confirming that he had died from head injuries sustained from being struck by motorcycle number 1876. The body was sent to the Pushan Villa for storage.

Continued Trial of the Huge Robbery Case Involving 120,000 Yuan 149

The major robbery of 129,080 yuan occurred at the entrance of Yong'an Fang on Xin Yong'an Street in the French Concession at 5:00 AM on the 16th of last month. Jin Jiulin, a supervisor from the French Concession Police Special Agency, and others, successively arrested the robbers Wang Maojian (aka Wang Rongchang), Zhang Weicai, Li Along (aka Scarface Along), and suspects Xu Wangshi (Wang Maojian's concubine), Zhang Yushi (Zhang Weicai's mother), and Huang Bosheng, six men and women in total. They recovered 46,675 yuan in stolen cash, which was sent to the Second Special Court for investigation. Arrest warrants were issued, with the approval of the French Police Department, for the remaining robbers: Da Luosong (aka Jiang Gaiyuan), Atu, Abao, and Patrolman Lao Si.

The previously arrested Wang Maojian and the other five individuals have been investigated by the police. It was discovered that Wang Maojian had committed a robbery in the Public Concession on June 3, 1926, and was sentenced to five years in prison. Zhang Weicai had also committed a robbery in the Public Concession on November 2, 1927, and was sentenced to three years in prison. Li Along had also committed theft and other crimes. All were repeat offenders. Yesterday afternoon, Wang Gangxu, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, heard the case in the First Criminal Court. The police lawyer, Fei Xizhen, presented the case, stating that the investigation revealed that the robbery was initiated by the two fugitives, Atu and Lanpiyan, who gathered the second, fifth, and sixth defendants, Wang Maojian, Zhang Weicai, and Li Along, and the fugitives Jiang Gaiyuan (aka Da Luosong) and one unknown accomplice. They met at the Jinliyuan Wharf on the morning of June 16th and decided to rob the large sum of money that the plaintiff Zhao Zhangyun was transporting from Wenzhou to Shanghai. Li Tu and Lanpiyan identified the car hired by the plaintiff and the old wooden box containing the money. They followed the car to the corner of Xin Yong'an Street on the Bund, where Jiang Gaiyuan (aka Da Luosong) and the other robbers used guns to intimidate and stop the car. The second, fifth, and sixth defendants seized the old box containing the money. Afterwards, they went to room 224 of the Da Shanghai Hotel at 348 Tianjin Road to divide the loot. The police are prosecuting the three robbers currently in custody, Wang Maojian, Zhang Weicai, and Li Along, for robbery with weapons by a group of three or more people under Article 348 of the Criminal Law. The police request that they be tried according to the law. The police have found that the first, third, and fourth defendants, Xu Wangshi, Zhang Yushi, and Huang Bosheng, are not related to the case and propose not to prosecute them. The police request a ruling on this matter. The police also presented the 8,475 yuan in stolen cash found in the homes of Xu Wangshi and others, as well as the receipt and guarantee of 38,200 yuan in stolen cash previously claimed by the plaintiff's representatives. Subsequently, the plaintiff's representatives, Xu Jinqing, Wang Xingshi, and Weng Laike, along with their attorney Yin Rubo, requested that the defendants be strictly pursued for the remaining unrecovered stolen money and that they be allowed to claim the stolen cash in custody. The court, after reviewing the statements, ordered the police to take down Xu Wangshi and the other two defendants, as the police were not prosecuting them. The three robbers Wang, Zhang, and Li were questioned separately (their statements were the same as before and are not recorded). The court then ordered the start of the debate, with the police lawyer and the lawyers Wu Kaisheng and Fan Gang, hired by the defendants, exchanging arguments. The court announced the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict for the 15th. The defendants were returned to the police station. Xu Wangshi, Zhang Yushi, and Huang Bosheng, who were not being prosecuted, were ordered to be released. The 8,475 yuan in stolen cash held by the police was ordered to be handed over to Zhao Zhangyun upon verification.

Analysis of Life Insurance Policies by Fei Mengfu 158

Life insurance takes legal effect through a contract (called a policy) between a life insurance company and the insured (generally known as the policyholder). The amount to be paid by the company is the face value of the policy, and the amount to be paid by the policyholder is the premium. It is necessary to have a large group of people seeking life insurance protection, so that the law of averages can be accurately applied, and the life insurance company can accurately know the amount of premiums to be paid by each policyholder. Therefore, to describe the operation of individual policies, it is necessary to assume that there is a large group of policyholders.

The Risks Borne by the Company

Suppose there are one thousand people aged thirty who simultaneously take out life insurance, with no savings feature specified on the policy, but hoping that one thousand yuan will be paid to their estate (beneficiary) after their death. The risk borne by the insurance company is one thousand times one thousand yuan, or one million yuan. If the company wants to collect the correct amount of premium, it needs to know when each person in this group will die. According to the life insurance mortality table, it is well known that not all of these one thousand people will die in the first year. However, it is certain and indisputable that the mortality rate in this group will increase year by year.

In the first year, eight of these thousand people will die. With such a simple calculation, it can be known that if the company charges each person eight yuan, it can guarantee one thousand yuan of life insurance for this thousand people for one year.

The Cost of Protection

At the beginning of the second year, this group will be short eight people, and the number of deaths will be higher, so the annual insurance cost will also be higher. The cost of protection increases every year until the age of the survivors reaches sixty or seventy, at which time the insurance for each person will inevitably be extremely high. Therefore, insurance companies should devise a strategy to allow each member of the group to equally distribute the cost of insurance over their lifetime. This can be achieved by charging a level premium. In this way, the amount collected in the early years will be higher than actually needed, so a reserve fund can be accumulated to prepare for future increases in mortality. Under a whole life policy, the policyholder continues to pay premiums for life, and if an accident occurs at any time, the insurance company immediately pays the face value of the policy to the policyholder's beneficiary.

Whole Life Policies

Let us discuss how this type of policy can protect policyholders against current dangers: First, this type of policy protects the policyholder's family. Therefore, when family protection is the main motive for insurance, this type of policy is always preferred. After the first premium has been paid, a large sum of cash property is immediately established. This amount is larger than what can be saved through other means over many years.

Cash Value

Second, the cash value of this type of policy increases year by year, until the policyholder reaches the normal retirement age (sixty or sixty-five), at which time they will have a substantial and absolutely certain fund in their life insurance policy. When the policyholder reaches old age, the need for family protection may be greatly reduced. Therefore, they can cancel most of their insurance and take back the cash value for their own use.

If the above-mentioned one thousand people do not wish to continue paying premiums for their insurance, but would rather pay higher premiums for a limited number of years, the company can issue limited-payment policies instead of whole life policies. In this case, premiums are only paid for the first ten, fifteen, or twenty years. Because the annual premium payable for this policy is higher than that payable for a whole life policy, its savings feature is obviously greater. The policyholder can accumulate a higher cash value in old age. This cash value can be withdrawn by the policyholder for their own purposes.

Savings Element

This group of policyholders may still feel unsatisfied. In addition to insurance protection, they want to include a larger savings element in the contract. They want to stop paying premiums at age fifty, sixty, or seventy and be able to receive a large sum of savings. The company can issue endowment policies to meet this need. Premiums are paid for ten, fifteen, twenty, twenty-five, or thirty years.

If the policyholder dies within the specified period, the company will pay the face value of the policy to their beneficiary. If the policyholder is still alive at the end of the period, the insurance money can be paid to the policyholder themselves.

Life Insurance Special Issue 159

Edited by the China Life Insurance Advancement Association

National Central Research Institute Letterhead

No. Page No.

Life Insurance is Savings

Using Money Wisely for the Future

The Best System for Protection

By Yang Ling

Republic of China, Date

Mr. Fei Mengfu, an American from Massachusetts, is a well-respected leader in the insurance industry in Shanghai. Immediately after graduating from Wesleyan University, he worked in the U.S. Army Medical Department, accompanying the expeditionary force to the French battlefield. After more than a year, when the European war ended, Mr. Fei went to the University of Edinburgh in England to continue his studies, focusing on philosophy. He was then hired by National Tsinghua University as a professor of philosophy and English. After three and a half years, he often enjoyed studying modern and ancient Chinese philosophy in his spare time. Deeply convinced that life insurance was essential for China, he changed his career to the insurance industry. In early 1922, he worked at American International Assurance Company. Facing numerous and complex tasks, he knew how to identify and appoint talent, and his planning was detailed and precise. In just a few years, the company's total insurance in force increased from nine million yuan to fifty-one million yuan, and Mr. Fei was promoted from a humble secretary to branch manager, assistant manager, and finally general manager.

Children's Education Insurance

The above points are the outlines of the three main types of life insurance contracts: whole life, limited payment, and endowment. These three types of contracts include the policies issued by various companies. Special contracts that meet specific needs are merely variations of these three main types of contracts. For example, a children's education insurance policy issued by a certain company is a type of endowment policy with a specific purpose. It creates a fund for future children's education expenses and dowries. Another type of

so-called three-benefit policy, a special contract, provides permanent protection for the policyholder's entire life, and also includes a savings feature, combining the principles of a limited-payment whole life policy and an endowment policy.

Four Essays on Life Insurance by Yu Ci 160

This article is written by Yu Ci, the current special advisor and honorary director of China United Life Insurance Company. Three articles have been published before this one. This is the fourth article, which discusses in detail how life insurance can promote social and economic welfare and the necessity of Chinese life insurance companies having expert guidance.

Life insurance is a profession that requires specialized talent, just like engineering, law, medicine, and other professions. Those engaged in the life insurance business who want to develop their business must have expert guidance, as discussed in the previous article. This article, in response to readers' requests, will explain the basic principles of life insurance as a profession and the qualifications required for life insurance actuaries. This is because the study of life insurance contains very deep mathematics, and it is quite difficult for those without mathematical training to understand the principles.

The origin of life insurance was mentioned in a previous article, where friends invited each other to pool money to provide for the surviving family members of the deceased. From this simple meaning, it gradually expanded to become the most important social organization today. Its benefits to society and people's livelihood cannot be measured by numbers. As a certain authority said, "In this time of global economic recession, society relies on this layer of protection, otherwise the consequences would be unimaginable."

As the life insurance industry gradually evolved from the nature of mutual assistance between individuals, the problems that needed scientific research to solve gradually arose due to the enlightenment of experience. The age problem is one of them. Except for those who die due to illness or accident, the higher the age, the closer they are to the end of their lives. Therefore, the amount of payment should be fairly distributed according to the age. Since the organization of life insurance companies, this payment, or what is now commonly called insurance premium, is determined and collected by the company according to the age of the policyholder, and the company fulfills the obligation to provide for the surviving family members of the deceased.

When this system was first implemented, life insurance companies only relied on the mortality statistics investigated by the government or public organizations as the standard for setting insurance premiums. However, this statistics is a general population census. In order to fairly calculate the insurance premium, people with poor health should not be allowed to take out life insurance, otherwise most of the insured will be weak people, and the mortality rate will inevitably increase. Since the insurance premium is determined according to this standard, it will inevitably be too high and beyond the individual's financial capacity.

After the above shortcomings were discovered, the applicant had to go through a selection procedure before confirming the initial method of organizing a selection committee dedicated to this matter, and then progressed to having doctors examine the physical condition; Today, the medical departments of various life insurance companies have become a very important part of the company because of their relationship with the prosperity of the business.

Since the establishment of the medical department, life insurance companies have gradually been able to create their own mortality statistics to replace the previously cited official statistics. The method is to collect materials supplied by most life insurance companies from their practical experience, analyze and sort them out, and make them. The first statistical table named "Life Insurance Calculation Method" or "Experience Integration" was published in 1843 AD, and the materials were supplied by seventeen British life insurance companies. The statistical table currently used in the United Kingdom is compiled by the London Life Insurance Calculation Society, and its materials are more detailed. The one currently used in the United States is still the "American Economic Life Insurance Statistical Table" published in 1868. In addition, there are also monographs on statistical tables specially compiled for tropical and subtropical countries.

After the above-mentioned statistical table, life insurance actuaries can use scientific methods to accurately calculate insurance costs without the drawbacks of leaning too much or too little. In addition to using the amount of insurance as a proportion, the amount of insurance premium must also be based on the age of the policyholder to see what the mortality rate is at this age. Without this statistics, there would be no accurate standard to follow. Although this does not mean that the insurance premium should increase every year because the policyholder is one year older and closer to death, if this is the case, the insurance premium will be higher and higher, which will inevitably be beyond the economic capacity of the insured. Life insurance companies that previously set insurance premiums according to this principle have all encountered failure. Later, the so-called "equal insurance premium level" system was adopted, that is, the insurance premium is determined first, and the same amount is used as the standard during the insurance period without increasing it. The basis of this system is to use the method of drawing from the surplus of the insurance premium in the first half of the insurance period to make up for the deficiency in the second half of the insurance period. The life insurance company collects this money and deposits it separately, extracting compound interest as a preparation for fulfilling its obligations in the future. This money is called the "deposit", which is the reserve that the life insurance company should have at any time. The nature of this reserve is so complex that the calculation of its amount should be sufficient to meet the needs, and it cannot be handled by non-professional actuaries.

Among all undertakings, none is more stable and more easily effective than the life insurance industry. To prove this with facts, the European War

and the post-war epidemic were rampant, and countless people died, but it has never been heard that life insurance companies have gone bankrupt as a result. Furthermore, in terms of the current situation, the world economy is in decline, and all industries are in depression, but the life insurance industry alone has made great progress. Tracing the cause, the life insurance industry is based on scientific principles, meets the needs of the times, and those engaged in this industry are mostly people with rich talents and knowledge, so the principles can be fully applied. Furthermore, due to the completeness of the life insurance laws in various countries, the interests of the public who invest in the life insurance industry are protected, so the life insurance industry can thrive.

The enactment of Chinese life insurance laws is only a matter of recent years, but this is also enough to prove that the life insurance industry is gradually being valued by society. Since the current law is newly created, it is difficult to compare it with other countries; however, it is not easy to improve it without the help of experts and borrowing from foreign countries. Therefore, this point may still be difficult to realize, and Chinese life insurance actuaries, because the life insurance laws of their own country are incomplete and cannot protect the public interest, need to have a deeper understanding of foreign life insurance laws. This point will be discussed further in the next issue of this special issue.

The Greatness of the American Insurance Industry by Da 161

We can imagine the astonishing greatness and importance of the insurance industry in the United States from the report of the New York State Department of Insurance. The assets accumulated by insurance companies of all levels approved to be established in New York State are no less than 32,491.36 million yuan, accounting for 10% of the total wealth of the United States. In 1930, their assets were more than this number, having reached as high as 32,900 million yuan. The reserves paid to the government by various companies over the years amounted to 9,000 million yuan by 1932. The assets of New York insurance companies are more than twice the U.S. national debt of 19,500 million yuan. The capital stock of each company

is now worth an average of more than 260 yuan per share.

The insured people of various types of insurance in the United States enjoy 10% of the total national wealth. Their financial resources, in addition to paying off the entire national debt, can also pay each person residing in the United States 100 yuan. If they want to withdraw these funds in cash immediately, it would require three and a half times the cash in circulation and in the treasury of the United States to be sufficient.

In 1932, life insurance companies throughout New York State had large amounts of premium income every day, because at that time most people needed insurance to secure their property and their lives, so the premiums paid to the companies by the insured people every day amounted to about 15 million yuan. At this time, the cash collected by various companies accounted for about 80% of the circulating currency. The application and need for this huge power can also be seen from the payments made to the insured people. In the same year, the total expenditure of the company due to death, fire, accidents, diseases, earthquakes, windstorms, economic panic, dividends, etc., was no less than 357.819 million yuan, which is nearly three-fifths of the circulating currency, averaging more than 11 million yuan per day (excluding Sundays). Even if the insurance companies only have the current assets, and there is no income from premiums and interest from various investments and mortgages in the future, they will be able to sustain the same losses as in 1932 for nine years without failing. Insurance managers have various fluent words and appropriate reasons, so that men, women, businesses, goods, etc. all have the need for insurance. Without the effect of this kind of effort, the company itself would not have accumulated and created this great power.

From the above statistics, we can recognize the power of the insurance industry in the United States and the greatness and importance of its mission.

Spring and Autumn

Defending the Clothing Front 162

— Wang Yansong

I am willing to lead the charge with a crossbow,

And I hope that my compatriots will provide support from the rear.

Reading the customs import statistics, I am saddened! The first item of imported goods is cotton cloth, and the eighth item is wool; these are all necessities for clothing for our compatriots. Like a tide and a mountain, no commodity can match them, while our country's silk, which is known for its beauty, is gradually declining, abandoning goods on the ground, and seeking help from others. Is this not the same as abandoning domestic chickens and preferring wild ducks? The country is weak and the people are poor, and it is appropriate that this should happen!

If commerce is called war, then today's merchants cannot be compared to those who only sought a profit of one in ten in the past. Since our country opened to trade, there has been commerce, but there has been no war. There has been war between merchants themselves, but there has been no war with foreign merchants. Foreign merchants take us as a market. Their national goods come in like entering an uninhabited land, while our merchants are guiding them every day, or slightly sharing their fodder as a stopover. Isn't this sad and shameful? In recent years, the stimulation has deepened, and concepts have changed. Patriotic psychology has gradually deepened, and merchants have also become well aware of the importance of promoting domestic goods, and domestic silk has shown vitality.

However, like a war, soldiers charge into battle as their duty, and the supply of military rations and the support of the masses are also necessary for victory. Today, when domestic silk battles with imported silk, silk merchants are soldiers on the front line, and the financial industry is the one who controls their rations, and the entire people are their only support from the rear. Only when the financial industry cooperates with the silk industry can the source of rations not be in short supply, and only when the entire people have something to wear, must they wear domestic products, and then the support from the rear will be solid. Yansong is unworthy, on the one hand, he is a soldier charging into battle, and on the other hand, he is also engaged in the military supply of providing rations. He dares not decline the charge with a crossbow. What I earnestly hope from my compatriots is that my compatriots will each fulfill the responsibility of supporting from the rear, so as to defend this clothing front. This is all I have to say.

The Rationalization of the National Silk Exhibition and the Future of National Silk (Part 1) 164

— Cheng Shouchong

From the customs statistics book, we can see that the export of silk is decreasing year by year, and the price of silk in the world market is also depreciating day by day. Domestic silk factories have no choice but to close down and stop work, creating a new record of terror. Because the international silk market has long been seized by violent Japan, and the farmers in the silk-producing areas have to continue to raise silkworms and cultivate mulberry trees with the concept of hoping for next year because of their livelihood. However, there is no Chinese financial organization abroad, and there is no direct foreign trade hub in China. The products are still sticking to the old ways, which leads to the inability to attract foreign customers, and the products are blocked in the domestic market. The only way out for weaving silk is only for a small number of Chinese people to enjoy. In addition, years of war and cheap grain hurt farmers, and brilliant foreign goods are rampant in our country with their dumping policies, and the sales of domestic silk have no place to stand. Silk cocoons are a major source of profit in domestic products. Once silk is stockpiled in the market, it will have a major impact on people's livelihood. If we don't plan for it early, silk will collapse and never recover. Now the silk industry has held a national silk exhibition to arouse the people to wear silk materials made in their own country. The mission it bears is not just for observation. It must be known that the psychological construction of adopting domestic products is in this one move; the great cause of reviving national silk is also in this one move! We should conduct large-scale tests on visitors to lay the foundation for revitalizing and improving national silk in the future. The method can be to print ready-made questions, or make a chart to be filled in by visitors, and let visitors understand that the national silk exhibition is not just for watching the excitement, but has a major mission to assist the silk industry, improve weaving, and consolidate the foundation, so that the source of profit of domestic silk is still in the hands of the Chinese people. Here are a few points:

(1) Testing

(1) The most suitable silk material;

(2) The most agreeable color;

(3) Which is more beautiful, printing or weaving?

(4) Do you like beauty or durability?

(5) Are the prices too low or too high?

(6) The gender, age, and occupation of the visitors.

(7) Which factory's products do you like the most?

(8) Which kind of goods has the fairest price?

By collecting and analyzing the above points, you can understand the psychology of customers. Therefore, the meaning of the exhibition is only to arouse customers' desire to buy and to distinguish national silk for exhibition. It is considered a non-fundamental exhibition. In order to develop the silk industry and promote the sales of products, we should base on the results of the tests to determine the business policy and weaving policy, take advantage of this opportunity of the national silk exhibition, and seek factual basis, and do not make guessing estimates with the action of a blind man riding a blind horse. Stop weaving products that do not meet the customer's psychology as soon as possible to avoid the danger of reducing consumption and stacking up.

Four Battalion Commanders of the Northeast 165

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eleven: Bowing the Head and Accepting Marriage, Fragrant Feelings Tenderly Caring, Delighting the Soldiers

Gui Zhi smiled at Man Ying and said, "So, in the future, Battalion Commander Tian will surely be promoted to Brigade Commander." Man Ying smiled faintly, without replying. That evening, it was late, and Ye Zhong stopped there, not continuing. The next day, Man Ying took the mother and daughter to see a talking movie. That evening, there was nothing to do, and they chatted idly in the house, and Mrs. Huang joined them. Madam Jiang said that she had left home for two or three days, and she was still a little worried. She would not go shopping in the market tomorrow and would return to Haidian early. Mrs. Huang held a water pipe in her hand, leaning towards them as she sat. She smoked two pipes of water, took out a handkerchief from her pocket, wiped the pipe mouth, then loaded a pipe of tobacco, held it with both hands, and handed it to Madam Jiang, smiling, "Have a pipe of water." Madam Jiang took the water pipe and said with a smile, "You people living in the city still smoke this?" Mrs. Huang said with a smile, "I'm used to smoking this, it's all the same, and it's much cheaper than smoking cigarettes." "Do they smoke water pipes in Haidian?" Madam Jiang said while smoking, "It's simply impossible to find one. Now the people outside the city are also learning to be fancy, what's not the same as in the city!" Mrs. Huang said, "You don't come to the city easily, do you?" Madam Jiang said, "Isn't that right? Miss Huang went to Haidian and said that the city is more prosperous than before, so our girl was happy for a while and insisted on coming! They dragged me along too, so I had to come and bother you for two days, and I should go back tomorrow." Mrs. Huang said, "Aren't you entrusting the old master of the Zhao family to watch over the house for you?" Madam Jiang said, "Yes. But after all, one can't always entrust others to take care of one's own family affairs." Mrs. Huang said, "Isn't Old Master Zhao a very nice person?" Madam Jiang said, "He's a very nice person. Battalion Commander Zhao is also a very nice person. Not to mention entrusting him to watch the door, even if it's something more important, it wouldn't matter to ask Old Master Zhao for help, but we're always embarrassed." Mrs. Huang said, "I heard our child say that Old Master Zhao still wants to arrange a marriage with your family, but it probably didn't work out, right?" (124)

Short Story

Beside the Eyebrow Pond 166

— Ke Ding'an

He woke up from his dream, turned on the electric light, and looked at the round gold clock on the small table. It was already half past three. He rubbed his eyes and warmed up his dream again...

He was sitting alone in his study, admiring her photo that she had personally given him. Just as he was missing her, she suddenly arrived gracefully. He was so happy that he jumped up and hurried over, holding her jade-like white hands, saying:

"Yue! You actually came, you actually came at this time, I was just missing you! I thought that being able to come at this time would be the most comforting thing for me, but unexpectedly, you actually came!"

"Ying! I was reading Mo Ruo's new poems alone, and I was so attracted by his poems that I felt very uneasy alone. At the same time, in my imagination, it seemed like someone was waiting for me. Who do you think this person waiting for me is?"

His face was red and he said...

"How would I know that! I think the person waiting for you must be the one you love the most!"

"That's right, that's exactly who I love the most! It's you, it's you..."

They could no longer restrain themselves, and their lips met.

Unexpectedly, a kitten, as if admiring their love, jumped in from the window silently. This jump was nothing, but it startled the harmonious couple. They thought someone was teasing them, so they separated and looked. It turned out to be just a kitten! They couldn't help but smile, but the kitten squatted at her feet, motionless.

They chewed on candy and chatted idly, from the vastness of the sky to the trivialities of the family. Finally, they discussed clothing. He said...

"Yue! You really agree with me. Since I graduated from senior primary school, I have abandoned all foreign goods for daily use and have not used them since. Although the import of foreign goods has increased unabated, I personally have not bought any of them. You are the same as me, which shows that our hearts are the same, don't you think?"

"My Ying! I think that we Chinese people, at a time when foreign insults are becoming more and more urgent, still don't know that everyone should use domestic goods. When it comes to that critical moment, I think there is absolutely no other way except to go to a dead end. Look at the so-called modern girls nowadays, who are afraid of not being modern every day. From head to toe, they deliberately research and create the elements that make them modern, and of course, they are all foreign goods. Don't you think this is a huge leak? If one person is like this, and millions of people are like this, it has caused a great panic in the Chinese silk industry. The biggest reason for this is the modern girls. In order to save China, we must first transform the hearts of modern girls, so that each of them has the determination to use domestic goods, then there will be a glimmer of hope!"

"The new cheongsam I'm making now is much better than foreign goods, and it will probably be finished tomorrow. Let's meet in Jingyuan and I'll show it to you."

Just at this moment, he suddenly woke up, and he tasted it as if he were eating olives.

After he woke up, the fresh flowers on the table seemed to have become more beautiful. He became even more excited and didn't want to sleep anymore. He opened the drawer, took out her photo, and stared at it in a daze.

Later, he saw her wearing a new dress in Jingyuan, made of light

green georgette, paired with slightly purple buttons, which further enhanced her charm. He suddenly remembered the scene in his dream last night.

Holding hands, they walked to the edge of the Eyebrow Pond and sat down side by side. He told her about the "dream."

"Ying! Your dream is so strange. This dress of mine is indeed newly made. The fabric was bought from the China National Goods Company. They have so many domestic silk fabrics! I wonder why people still want to use foreign silk!"

"Yue! Chinese silk has so many modern patterns, I always want to think of a wonderful way to advise them..."

Before she could finish speaking, her eyes were fixed on the pond, where a pair of mandarin ducks were quietly resting with their wings together. They also imitated them in the same way.

Ministry of Education Approves Jiangsu Education Department to Implement Primary School Regulations with Flexibility 171

The Ministry of Education, based on a report from the Jiangsu Education Department, stated that there were four points of difficulty in implementing the Primary School Law and Primary School Regulations: "㈠ Article 16 of the Primary School Law stipulates that primary schools shall not charge tuition fees, but may collect a reasonable amount based on local conditions in public primary schools, with a maximum of one yuan per semester for elementary grades and a maximum of two yuan for higher grades. Articles 65 and 66 of Chapter 11 of the Primary School Regulations also have very strict regulations regarding the collection of tuition fees in primary schools. Article 68 of the same chapter also stipulates that primary schools shall not charge children

miscellaneous fees. The Ministry is actively promoting compulsory education, considering the hardships of the people, but it has been found that most primary schools in various counties in Jiangsu Province collect tuition fees as a principle, and the tuition fees are included in the budget as legitimate income. The amount of collection is carefully determined based on the local living standards and the situation of the people. Generally, the smaller amount is similar to the standard stipulated in the Primary School Law, and the larger amount, such as in Wujin, Wuxi, Jiangyin, and other counties, is four to six yuan per semester for higher grades and two to four yuan per semester for elementary grades.

This is several times higher than the standard stipulated in the Primary School Law. In the above-mentioned counties, the tuition income in the budget is around 100,000 yuan. If it is suddenly changed to collect according to the Primary School Law, the legitimate income will be greatly reduced. Before there is a way to compensate for this, it will be necessary to suspend some grades, which is contrary to the purpose of popularization. Furthermore, although primary schools in various provinces and counties do not formally include miscellaneous accommodation fees in the budget, they often rely on this fee to subsidize office expenses and repair school buildings. In total, it is about 150,000 yuan per year in the province. If it is abolished all at once, the government will have to find a way to subsidize it, otherwise it will be difficult to maintain the progress of the business, and the indirect impact will not be small. Considering the above two points, at a time when disasters are frequent and financial resources are exhausted, and it is impossible to actively prepare for compensation, it is proposed to temporarily maintain the current situation in the province and gradually reduce the amount of collection in the future, so as to comply with the regulations. ㈡ The Primary School Regulations stipulate that the number of students in each class should be 40, with a minimum of 25. This seems to be a slightly wider restriction compared to the provincial regulations of 50 students per class, with a minimum of 30. The province's economy and strength are extremely restricted. Regarding the number of students, please allow us to temporarily follow the provincial standard. ㈢ Article 11 of the Primary School Law stipulates that the principals of county, city, district, meritorious, or township primary schools shall be selected and recommended by the county and city education administrative organs and submitted to the county and city governments for appointment, and shall be submitted to the education department for record. Furthermore, the principals of affiliated primary schools shall be hired by the principals of the managing schools and submitted to the managing education administrative organs for record. The above two regulations are slightly different from the current methods in the province. Principals of county primary schools in the province have always been selected by the county education bureaus in accordance with the regulations and submitted to the county for reporting to the education department for approval, and then appointed by the county government. Although this is not without twists and turns, it was originally intended to be cautious in the selection of personnel, and in principle, it does not violate the Primary School Law, and it seems that it can still be implemented. After a part of the provincial middle schools in the province implemented the independent normal school system and were changed into normal schools, the original experimental primary schools of each middle school were also changed into affiliated primary schools of the normal schools. The persons in charge were changed from principals to directors, but qualified personnel were still selected by the principals of the normal schools and submitted to the education department for approval, in order to preserve the spirit of independence, which is implicitly in line with the purpose of the Primary School Regulations. It is proposed that on the one hand, the title should be immediately changed to principal, and on the other hand, qualified personnel should still be selected and recommended by the principals of the normal schools and submitted to the department for appointment, so that they can be兼任. ㈣ The Primary School Regulations stipulate that the county and city education administrative organs may designate one primary school in each school district as the central primary school, but shall not indicate the word "central" in the school name. It has been years since Jiading, Jinshan, and other counties in Jiangsu Province implemented the central primary school district system, especially the facilities in Jiading, which have achieved considerable results. The method is to abolish the education committees and select a complete primary school with excellent performance and a central location in each district to be designated as the central primary school. In addition to fully providing the research results for the reference and implementation of the primary schools in the district and actively supervising them, the principal also has the administrative power of the education committee. The only difference from the Primary School Regulations is that it avoids the name of "central." It is believed that the current central primary school district system in Jiangsu Province has already achieved results, and its purpose is only a matter of name. If the central school loses its ties due to the trivial matter of changing its name, and the hard-earned harvest in the past is completely lost, it seems regrettable. It is proposed to allow it to continue to be implemented on an experimental basis, in order to see its success." Please examine the actual situation and allow temporary flexibility, etc., and then order the department to say, "After checking, the points presented are factual. For the first point, due to the difficulty in raising funds for a while, it is approved to continue to handle it as before, but funds should be raised in the next two years to compensate and reduce the amount of collection, so as to comply with laws and regulations. For the second point, the minimum number of students stipulated in the Primary School Regulations shall not be changed. The original intention of the regulations is not violated by the number of students exceeding 40, and it should be approved. The original intention of the regulations is also not violated by the third point. The fourth point is of a testing nature and should be allowed to be flexible."

Soochow Law School Improves Academic System 179

Since its establishment on Kunshan Road in Shanghai, the Soochow University Law School has produced many talented individuals, making it the only specialized law school in China. Now, the school is making further improvements to its academic system. Starting next semester, it will be divided into day and night schools. The day school will only admit high school graduates, who will graduate in four years. The first year will focus on social sciences, while the second to fourth years will focus on law and social sciences. The second-year level will still be located within the Soochow Arts and Sciences College, with branches in both Shanghai and Suzhou. The third and fourth years will be entirely located in Shanghai. The night school program will remain the same for the time being, but starting in the autumn of 1934, it will only admit students who have graduated from domestic and foreign universities, with a three-year graduation period. In addition, there will be a three-year postgraduate program. It is heard that the school will begin enrolling new second-year students for the day school and third-year students for the night school after the summer vacation.

Hubbelden's New Tennis Champion: Crawford Defeats Barnes in the Final 184

4-6, 11-9, 6-2, 2-6, 7-5

Australian Player Wins Championship After Eleven Years

Barnes' Cannonball Serve Ultimately Breaks Down

(Reuters, London, 7th) Australian champion Jack Crawford defeated defending champion Barnes of the United States 4-6, 11-9, 6-2, 2-6, 7-5 in the men's singles final at the Hubbelden Tennis Championships today to win the 1933 Hubbelden New Championship.

First Time in Eleven Years 185

This is the first time an Australian player has won the championship since Paterson won the Hubbelden Championship in 1922. It has been eleven years since then. Today's game was held in the hot sun, and the number of spectators increased day by day, and today's number should break the previous record.

Victory Lies Entirely in the Second Set 186

The battle between Crawford and Barnes for the championship aroused the enthusiastic interest of the audience. The Australian champion's wonderful hitting technique was unprecedented. The key to his victory was in the second set, where Barnes's terrifying cannonball serve was broken. Crawford replied with explosive shots, which he had never done before. This set lasted for three quarters of an hour, and the server won the game until the 20th game, when Barnes's serve was broken by Crawford. Crawford finally won 11-9, making it 1-1.

Fierce Battle in the Final Set 187

Crawford won the second set very easily, but the loss in the fourth set was similar. In the final set, both sides fought to the death, and the servers won the game again.

Until 5-5, Crawford broke Barnes's almost irresistible violent serve again, winning a crucial game with a sliding four. Finally, Crawford's serve was successful, and Crawford won again and won the championship. The cheers shook the clouds for three minutes.

Bai Lang's "Tennis Tips," Translated by Wu Bangwei, Published Today 191

Tennis practitioners must read it

The Qinfen Bookstore, opposite the Chinese Sports Association on Father Laoshu Road in Shanghai, has published "Tennis Training," "Tilden's Tennis Technique," and "The Secret of Winning by World Tennis Players" in the Sports Series, which are popular in the world. Now, Wu Bangwei, a lecturer at the Ministry of Education's Summer Sports Remedial Class, has translated "Tennis Tips" written by Ms. Bai Lang, the American women's singles and doubles champion. The book is divided into 22 chapters, including introduction, tennis secrets, hitting essentials, footwork and movements, backhand hitting, return balls and net balls, timing of hitting, spin and slice, serve, center of gravity movement, smash, volley, return high ball method, sideline draw, on-court essentials, lunge, changes in position and angle, doubles strategy, singles strategy, head-to-head competition and psychology, and racket selection. The author has profound observations and research on the advantages of world-renowned tennis players. The content of this book is a collection of the achievements of various schools. All beginners and experienced tennis players must read it. In addition to the smooth text and exquisite printing, the book has various competition method diagrams and more than 50 hitting photos of Tilden, Madame Madi, Blogs, Puckster and other world tennis players. Readers can see the training methods at a glance. In order to popularize the book, it is only sold for 70 cents, with a special price of 10% off. If you send a letter to purchase, the registered postage is 11 cents. The bookstore's store at 554 Sima Road will be on sale at the same time from today.
