Free Talk

Suspicion Breeds Dark Demons 197

— Cao Zhouren

In the past, being limited by teachers to write essays was very painful because there was nothing to say. Now that I can write essays freely and without any subject, it is still very painful; there are many people with mental illnesses who read articles, and suspicion breeds dark demons, and they see thorns that ridicule them from the gaps between the words. When Mr. Lu Xun's "The True Story of Ah Q" was published as an appendix in the Jingbao, "many people were trembling with fear, fearing that they would be scolded in the future. And a friend said to me (Hanlu) in person that a certain paragraph in yesterday's "The True Story of Ah Q" seemed to be scolding himself. Therefore, he guessed that "The True Story of Ah Q" was written by someone, why? Because only someone knew about his private affairs. … When he found out the author's name, he realized that he did not know the author at all, and therefore, he suddenly realized himself, and then declared to everyone that he was not being scolded." (Hanlu Idle Talk) Fortunately, the author and the person with mental illness did not know each other, otherwise Mr. Lu Xun would have been wronged. We are born into this world, and it is inevitable to close our noses and sneeze; but it is also mostly written casually, without any deep meaning, and those with mental illnesses must say that it is ridiculing him, so the person who writes feels the pain of writing and the difficulty of finding a topic at all times! When "The True Story of Ah Q" was included in "A Call to Arms", someone asked Mr. Lu Xun: "Who exactly are you scolding?" Mr. Lu Xun could only say with grief and indignation: "I regret that I cannot make people see that I am not so inferior!"

Yesterday I read the "Two Kinds of Autumn Rain Cottage Notes", in which a passage quoted many poems from predecessors. For example, the poem chanting the waterfall says·· "Flowing to the former stream without a word, making many sounds in the mountain." For example, the poem chanting the iron horse says: "What is the matter with the tinkling sound? It is the people under the fence who are not happy." For example, the poem chanting the summer cloud says: "Infinite drought seedlings are dying, leisurely making strange peaks." For example, the poem chanting the cicada says: "Don't rely on high branches to sing loudly, you should also look back at the praying mantis." These poems are good because they were written by the ancients. If they were written by Mr. Lu Xun, I don't know how many people would be blushing and thinking that they were talking about his privacy. The wise and holy emperor is on top, and "the breeze does not know the words, why is it flipping through books indiscriminately" has the misfortune of being beheaded. The literary inquisition was originally decorating the prosperous age of peace!

If you want people to have no mental illness, even Freud has no way to do it. Although it is a bit painful, let's improve the writer's side. In the past, there were two secrets to being a doorman under the famous dukes, giants, and wealthy households. The first one is to always say "You look very good, and you've been getting better lately!" If he asks us to estimate his age, estimate a forty-year-old to be thirty years old, and a fifty-year-old to be forty years old. Although it is a smile, his joy is known. The second type is that if he buys antiques or collects calligraphy and paintings, estimate fifty dollars to be one hundred dollars, and estimate one hundred dollars to be one hundred and fifty dollars. Don't estimate too much, which shows that you are an amateur, and never estimate too little, which shows that he is an amateur. And you must have something to say, seven parts praise and three parts criticism, which is exactly what he likes. This is what Mr. Feng Zhiyu called "the art of three ugliness". If we want to avoid people's "suspicion breeding dark demons", we can only improve it in this way.

However, the love song "The Reeds and White Dew" has a preface saying that it "刺襄公也，未能用周禮，將無以固其國焉" (sarcastic of Duke Xiang, because he failed to use the Zhou ritual, he will not be able to secure his country). When there are too many interpretations by virtuous people, even the places that the saint does not take seriously will jump out with a satirical meaning; we only pray that the virtuous people who make interpretations will be merciful... because the man who wants to love does not care about these "Zhou rituals"!

The Method of Preserving Life 198

— Xu Maoyong

Recently, writers are prone to disappear, and once they disappear, they become a "happy ending". In such a world, it is really necessary to pay attention to the method of preserving life.

I accidentally flipped through a thread-bound book and got Chen Meigong's method, which I immediately made public to the world, saying: "The superior man closes his heart, the middle man closes his mouth, and the inferior man closes his door."

The plan of closing the door is clumsy and obvious, because staying at home easily arouses suspicion, or is thought to be holding secret meetings, or is thought to be making bombs. Moreover, as the saying goes: "Sitting at home with the door closed, disaster comes from the sky", which has long revealed the unreliability of closing the door.

Confucius entered the temple of Houji and sealed the mouth of the golden man with three seals. As the saying goes, "是非只爲多開口" (trouble only comes from talking too much), so it is important to close your mouth. Ruan Sizong "does not criticize people", and once got drunk for two months, refusing Sima's marriage proposal, and deeply understands the way to close his mouth, so he was able to avoid the same mistakes as Ji Kang, and can be used as a model, but there are still some improprieties.

Those are his eighty-two poems of nostalgia. Although these poems are said to be "difficult to measure with emotion after a hundred generations", Chen Hang made a note, saying that many of them use "妾婦" (concubine) to mock Sima, and "膏火" (grease) to compare villains. Fortunately, Chen Hang was not at the same time as Sizong, otherwise, if these words were spread to Sima and his subordinates, could Ruan Ji still "善終" (die well)?

People who want to write poems of nostalgia do so because their hearts are too sensitive. Even if the "言至玄遠" (words are mysterious and distant), they must beware of "索隠" (searching for hidden meanings) families. Therefore, the superior man is able to close his heart.

Mr. He Ru has given an example of closing the heart, that is, Ren Yong of the Later Han Dynasty, who saw his wife committing adultery in front of him, hid the truth and said nothing, and saw his son fall into a well, but endured and did not save him.

But can you do it?

Another Fire Thief 199

— Ding Meng

The source of fire, the Greeks thought, was stolen from the sky by Prometheus, so he angered the great god Zeus, who chained him to a high mountain and ordered an eagle to peck at his flesh every day.

The Wawanganti people of Africa also use fire, but it was not taught to them by the Greeks. They have another fire thief.

People cannot know the name of this fire thief, or it has long been forgotten. He stole fire from the sky and passed it on to the ancestors of the Wawanganti people. Therefore, he angered the great god Daras. This passage is similar to the ancient Greek legend. But Daras's method was different. He did not lock him on the mountain peak, but secretly locked him in a dark cellar, without letting anyone know. What was sent was not an eagle, but mosquitoes, fleas, and bed bugs, sucking his blood while making his skin swell. At this time, there were also flies, who were the best at finding wounds, buzzing and sucking desperately, and then pulling a lot of fly dung on his skin to prove what an unclean thing he was.

However, the Wawanganti people did not know this story. They only knew that fire was invented by the chief's ancestors and used by the chief to burn heretics and burn down houses.

Fortunately, transportation is now developed, and some African flies have also flown to China. I heard this little bit from their buzzing.

The Sorrow of the Middle Class 200

— Another Realm

When the poor reach the point where they have no pants to wear, the rich bosses are naturally worried, but fortunately there is still a middle class in society. Although it has become pitifully dry, it still has some oil and water compared to those who have no pants to wear. The greedy eyes of the rich bosses are shining on them.

They want to cry, but they still want to get rich, and they still want women. The rich bosses may understand this better than they do themselves. He extends the most tempting and stimulating giant spirit, not afraid that these middle classes will not fall into the net;

"You can turn stones into gold with just a little effort!"

"This is the time to explore the naked palace!"

Young masters naturally don't care about this 18,000, the poor still can't afford this pack of cigarettes that costs more than a dozen copper coins, the idle long gown class and the small businessmen with tears in their eyes are waiting day and night for such a windfall, their economic ability is only enough to blow the ashes of this kind of cigarette, and from then on they will work harder to blow, "It hasn't been a month… it's already been given away", so here come another 500,000 numbers.

On the other hand, we are told, "Up and down are full, please come early tomorrow!" Naturally, the patrons here are still those friends who are neither up nor down.

However, even if the picture is more naked, it is still empty. There is no way but to "seek a good partner" and "seek a son-in-law", I am afraid that no matter "I only seek a gentle nature, regardless of poverty" and "Regardless of whether you are married or unmarried", the results will always be difficult to achieve.

As expected, it only takes a little effort, but the miracle of turning stones into gold cannot fall on everyone's head. The stomach cannot always be empty, and you still have to drag a broken gown. Fortunately, the newspaper has recently been willing to give people "self-employment introductions" without advertising fees, so there are dozens of them appearing every day. Those with literary talent can also write a "special self-employment introduction". However, the cold reality will simply not listen to your thorough complaint, it doesn't need anything from you except to turn the "stone" into the rich boss's gold vault!

Most of the commercial advertisements in the newspaper every day are almost all expressions of the rich bosses' clever exploitation of the middle class, and at the same time there are equal pages printed with the weak moans of those who are being exploited!

The sorrow of the middle class will continue to extend until its demise!

A Most Recent Discovery 201

— Jiang Zhisheng

Two months ago, I happened to hear friends talking about something called "Liberation Lyrics" and the big name of a certain Mr. Zeng, and I thought it was just an ignorant and reckless person trying to show off. As a result, he was met with rebukes from all sides, perhaps he already deeply regrets trying to be clever and failing? At that time, I thought people like Mr. Zeng were just laughable.

Later, I unintentionally ran into a certain gentleman familiar with the inside story of the Shanghai literary and art circles, and after listening to his words, I finally realized that the rebukes from all sides regarding "Liberation Lyrics" not only did not prompt Mr. Zeng to reflect, but instead made him elated; because when people scolded "Liberation Lyrics," they would bring up Mr. Zeng's name, and Mr. Zeng could use this to become famous. There are originally people in the world who are accustomed to putting on a clown's face, making grand pronouncements and jokes everywhere, and as a result, they become famous. Mr. Zeng is just one of the youngest among them. So I felt that this person was really boring and shameless.

The day before yesterday, I suddenly saw Mr. Cui Wanqiu's advertisement in the Shen Bao and the records in the fifth issue of Sino-Foreign Books and Newspapers, exposing Mr. Zeng's private affairs, saying how he borrowed the names of friends to brag about himself, and how he spread rumors to slander his friends. Oh! Such a thing happened! So I felt that Mr. Zeng was not only boring and shameless, but simply sinister and terrible!

I remember when people criticized "Liberation Lyrics" before, a friend said; the "Liberation Lyrics" like "playing mahjong" are just like a pug wagging its tail, trying to get a smile from the ladies after dinner and drinks. Neither the person nor his words deserve to be criticized. Now I know that the pug's mouth actually has poisonous teeth, and it will bite people unexpectedly, even secretly biting the hand that feeds it bread. Inherently flawed types are originally not limited to just one or two, and there are probably still many hidden in the literary and art circles. If you are not careful, you will be sold out. No wonder my friend, Mr. So-and-so, warned his son not to think about becoming a writer. These are truly experienced words. Mr. So-and-so's passive approach is actually not feasible. People in the literary and art circles should work hard to do a cleanup to maintain the purity of the literary world. At least, they should post a few more slogans;

"Beware of pugs with poisonous teeth!"

Creative Novel

Ordinary Matters (6) 202

— Dan Guosun

"Fifth Brother Shi," Bo Tang said, "You are too worried. Do you think they will detain people?"

"Whether they detain him or not is secondary," Pei Yu said, "It's always good to be cautious."

"Then, Bo Tang, why don't you make a phone call and ask him to come here first thing tomorrow morning?"

"Great," Pei Yu urged Bo Tang, "Go make the call!"

Bo Tang was a little annoyed and said, "No need."

"What if something really goes wrong?" Pei Yu said, "If you don't go, then I will!"

"His phone is borrowed from next door. It's so late now, everyone is already asleep, who would be willing to call Zhi Guang to listen to the phone for you?..."

"Then call first thing tomorrow morning!" Pei Yu said.

"Isn't that the same as no one being willing to do it... If you really want him to come, just have A Ming take the car to pick him up early tomorrow morning!"

This accidentally gathered meeting of relatives and friends passed such a proposal.

Around seven o'clock, A Ming drove the car to Cai Shi Road to pick up Zhi Guang, but Zhi Guang had already gone to the factory in Da Nanmen. A Ming rushed to the factory and found out that Zhi Guang had already left with several workers, and no one knew where they had gone; the situation in the factory was not tense, because there was no work to do, so there were not many workers.

Bo Tang's residence was on the south side of the road, standing at the wrought iron gate, looking south along the cement path inside the gate... on the left, a row of locust trees connected to the branches of the neighbor's trees outside the wall, and on the right, a French-style two-story gray-white western-style building; however, what you see first is the rear section of that western-style building. Twenty steps further ahead, there is a semi-circular stone staircase made of five or six stone steps, closely connected to the entrance of the L-shaped corridor downstairs, walking around the corner of the corridor and then south is the front porch of the building, and in front of the porch there is also a stone staircase, long, square, and high, facing the lawn more than an acre wide in front of the building. Although the color of the grass only shows a withered yellow shadow, such an area, matched with the long doors and long windows of the two south-facing halls downstairs, is also very rich in harmonious meaning. These two halls are of course where Bo Tang has always entertained guests; but now, not only have the two halls been converted into the main part of his temporary shelter for those relatives, friends, and refugees, with all the furnishings moved away; but even in the passage behind the hall, which forms the main artery of transportation in the rear of this western-style building, many floor mats have to be opened at night, so when A Ming jumped out of the car and walked up the semi-circular stone steps to open the doors on both ends of the passage facing the stairs, he still saw the heads of many maids and older sisters, half-hidden and half-visible in several comforter covers on the ground.

He tiptoed slowly from the gaps in the stalls of people lying like salted fish to the side of the handrail on the north side of the passage, just about to step up one or two steps, when he heard his female owner asking from the handrail upstairs...

"Is that A Ming? Has Mr. Zhang been picked up?"

A Ming reported the facts again. Pei Yu asked...

"Does no one in the factory really know? Have you asked carefully?"

"Asked," A Ming said, "No one knows, I think they took a rickshaw towards the public building, so it will naturally be slower."

Financial: Little Increase in Silver Prices, Gold Pricing Process Extremely Monotonous 203

Midway Covering Shorts Once Saw a Momentary Advance

Ultimately Headwinds of Selling Caused Prices to Fall Again

After the previous day's sharp decline in the gold market, yesterday was quite calm. Midway, covering shorts was eager and prices rose at one point, but ultimately, due to the bank's squeeze and headwinds of selling, prices still fell. The situation is uncertain. In the early morning, due to the drop in the electrical London silver price and the rise in the American silver price, the forward silver price on the Gold Exchange only rose by two and a half and one and three-tenths of a penny, which was not satisfactory. In addition, American cotton fell by nineteen pounds and American wheat also shrank by more than one cent. Stocks rose slightly, and people's minds seemed stable, but because the British and American exchange rates rose sharply by two dimes and two cents, and the American and British exchange rates rose by one dime, one cent, and one-eighth of a cent, they failed to open high. If the increase in British and American and American and British exchange rates were reversed, then prices would continue to fall. The gross plate initially made thirty-two yuan, then retreated to twenty-five yuan. After opening, with large households like Bing Xing aggressively covering shorts, it rose sharply at one point, and the HSBC listed American exchange rate increased by another half yuan due to squeezing exchange rates. The road to rising was greatly hit. Soon, the exchange market loosened and the situation went downstream. The process during the morning was mediocre, and the result was a slight increase. Under the combined calculation of the strength of the American silver price increase and the American and British exchange rate, it was felt that it shrank a lot. When the American silver price was the same price before, the gold pricing was outside of eight hundred and eighty yuan, so the gold market's sentiment turned better and the future was still uncertain. The cooked red price was increased by one hundred and sixty-six yuan. The situation of the morning market is recorded as follows:

The opening in the morning was eight hundred and thirty yuan, slightly higher than the previous close of two yuan and three cents. The material opened at zero and five cents. Private Estimate of U.S. Cotton 212

New York, 7th Dispatch: The Texas Cotton Bureau estimates this year's cotton acreage at 40,183,000 acres, with production conditions at 71.9% of normal, and a yield of 13,725,000 bales.

Dry Weather Creates Uncertainty in U.S. Cotton Market 213

New York, 7th Dispatch: A report on the cotton market for the week states that at the beginning of the week, President Roosevelt's decision to raise domestic prices caused the dollar to plummet, and the continued drought in the Southwest led to active buying and new price peaks. However, this also triggered a reaction, and the destruction of cotton fields is proceeding rapidly. The northwest of Texas has also received heavy rain. The government's first count of sown acreage as of July 1 will be the basis for the destruction. The result will depend on the impact of the reduction movement. The cotton market is firm, but trading is limited. Both supply and demand sides are uncertain about values, and seem to be waiting for the development of cotton spinning regulations, handling fees, and cotton production reduction. At the same time, the authorities' monetary and economic policies are also limiting the market.

Recently, teas from Tunxi, Suian, and Wuyuan have been selling very well. Yesterday, British companies Xiehe and Yihua began to actively purchase local Zhenmei tea due to demand from French companies. The green tea market appears to be stable. The situation is still difficult to consider optimistic.

Home Life Special Issue

The True Happiness of Life 221

— Pu

In the "Slum Life Special Issue" of this journal, Issue No. 26, the reporter mentioned our motive and hope in publishing that special issue. This time, the publication of this "Home Life Special Issue" requires even more explanation. We respectfully seek the guidance of our readers.

We firmly believe that the vast majority of readers of this journal, in this national group where illiteracy accounts for more than 80%, are still in the position of the literate class. Our environment can also be said to be living a life that is far from being enough (comfortable home) and more than enough (slum). We may be worthy of the title of "middle class"? Or some people question the permanence of this so-called "middle class". We believe that the length of this class is not what we want to argue, but in the current situation, under the lifeless state of the entire nation, especially in the semi-colonial environment of Shanghai, we feel that those who deeply feel the pain of oppression and who are the most energetic, courageous, and determined to strive for the equality of human life are still this so-called "middle class." Because they are also oppressed, and at the same time, they understand the reasons for this oppression better than their compatriots in the slums. We believe that for the future revitalization of the Chinese nation and the transformation of the entire social system, this so-called "middle class" is the sharpest and most sensitive tool. Although we know the strengths of this class, we should also know the general biggest shortcomings of this class, that is, it is very easy to change its mind halfway, be fickle, and lack the spirit of hard work. The reason for this shortcoming is mostly due to the relationship of the past environment. Isolation of the lives of the majority of the laboring masses, lack of empathy, lack of sense of responsibility, unclear path of transformation, on the other hand, it is dazzled by the comfort of home life, tempted by individual hedonism, does not understand the principle of human evolution and the creation of mutual assistance, and does not have the correct meaning of life. Regarding the former aspect, the reporter has briefly discussed it in the "Slum Life Special Issue" of Issues 26 and 27. What we want to discuss today is the latter aspect.

We silently observe a kind of "foolish and content" expression of most of the hard-working masses in the country, as well as the most leisurely enjoyment of the various material pleasures created and invented by foreigners from the results of mutual assistance and effort, and we will sometimes feel the fear that this ancient nation will decline and perish. Although our voice is very weak, we will never give up. We want to cry out loudly to arouse the awareness of compatriots with aspirations to save the country and a few who enjoy a comfortable home life. If this personal-centered attitude towards life does not change, then all other tunes for saving the country and the people will not be able to be played!

The first thing to be brought up for discussion is whether people who enjoy a comfortable home life can get the true happiness of life? Even if we take a step back from an individual point of view, we know that so-called happiness is just a comparative term. For example, "peace" comes from a comparison of movement. If there is no movement at all, then there is no feeling of "peace". As for "happiness", it comes from a comparison of suffering. If you don't encounter the problem of "suffering" or pursue "suffering", then even if there is so-called "happiness", it is very superficial and monotonous. The "peace and happiness" that the enjoyers of this kind of life can get is definitely not as interesting as the bystanders imagine and guess. In fact, according to what we know, there are many enjoyers of comfortable home life who feel that life is boring and painful because of excessive "peace and happiness". Moreover, people are not only animals that can use their hands, but also animals that can use their brains to think and seek progress in the environment. We probably all know that thinking and studying problems with our brains is not a happy thing. We easily envy the happiness of an inventor who invented something, but we often do not pay attention to the various hardships he has gone through before the invention. Therefore, a person's true happiness is to seek "peace" in movement, to gain "happiness" in suffering, and to seek happiness from the "progress" of overcoming difficulties and pain. We believe that this is the true happiness of life. We ask, can the true meaning of this happiness be understood by ordinary enjoyers of comfortable home life?

Shuttle 222

— Little Dull

Daily Life of a Rich Family

丨This material is based on the description of a nanny, but slightly整理丨

The ladies have finished playing cards, and the young master and young lady have returned from dancing! "Knock knock!" The door was knocking like thunder, and I, who was so tired that I couldn't open my eyes, had to squint and grope my way out to open the door.

"Damn it! Why so slow?" The young master scolded as he opened the door.

Leather shoes and high-heeled leather shoes walked upstairs, clattering.

×　×　×　×　×

Six o'clock; seven o'clock... Twelve o'clock, the sun is hanging in the middle. The lady has slept enough. "Nanny, the opium tray." After lighting the lamp, preparing the pipe, and placing it properly, I carried it upstairs. "Chi chi..." The lady smoked opium. The master woke up. "Nanny, face water." After pouring the face water, I took it upstairs and placed it.
